Factors causing Mental issues could be Personal, Financial, Social, Professional or Physical ??? Could be any one or many of these factors.

Mental health is such a strong factor that can make or break a person. so be Positive, think positive and Enjoy this beautiful journey...Called Life.

27/09/23, 2:06â€¯pm - Aai: RC - RAJASTHAN MARWAD
7 Days 6 Hotel Nights

Rajasthan: Bikaner 2N, Jaisalmer 2N (Hotel 1N + Desert Camp 1N), Jodhpur 2N

Visit: 3 Cities 1 Country
1Jaipur - Bikaner
Arrive at the designated reporting place, report to vehicle and proceed to Bikaner. The Marwad portion of Rajasthan lies partly in Thar Desert. In Sanskrit the word 'maru' means desert and 'wad' refers to region, so the word 'Marwad' literally means 'The region of Desert'. With a long, rich history and heritage and sand dunes just close by, it's not surprising that Bikaner is also called â€œCamel Countryâ€ .

Extra Topping : Tea/ Coffee enroute Jaipur to Bikaner journey

Dinner
2Bikaner
Enjoy city tour of Bikaner which includes visit to Deshnok Rat temple â€“ A unique Temple dedicated to Karni Mata of Deshnok, Junagarh Fort - one of the most decorated forts in India and houses opulent palaces that give you a peek into the lives and times of the maharajas of Bikaner. Here we also see Anup Mahal, Gaj Mandir, Sheesh Mahal, Prachina Museum, Sadul Museum. Visit Asia's biggest Camel Research Farm - where you get a chance to encounter different camel breeds. Later we view the magnificent Lalgarh Palace. Later enjoy the puppet show - An ancient art form of Rajasthan.

Extra Topping : Bikaneri Bhujiya & Tea/ Coffee/ Soft Drink at Karni Mata Temple. Tea / Coffee / Kulfi at Camel Research Farm.

Breakfast
Lunch
Dinner
3Bikaner â€“ Jaisalmer
Proceed to Jaisalmer â€“ nicknamed as the Golden city because the yellow sandstone used throughout the architecture of both the fort and the town. On arrival enjoy Camel ride, folk dance and magnificent sunset at the famous Sam Sand Dunes with dinner.

Extra Topping : Tea / Coffee en-route to Jaisalmer.

Notes: Air Cooler Tents will be provided at Jaisalmer Desert Camp.

Breakfast
Lunch
Dinner
4Jaisalmer - Desert camp Jaisalmer
Morning enjoy city tour of Jaisalmer which includes visit to Jaisalmer Fort also known as Golden Fort - A UNESCO World Heritage Site and the most prominent landmarks of the city, Jain Mandir, Patwan ki Haweli and museum - with its unique intricate carvings, architecture and design is one of the most significant Havelis in Jaisalmer and Rajasthan and Nathmalaji ki Haweli - an ornate architecture in the heart of the city. Later enjoy boating at the beautiful Gadisar Lake. In the evening enjoy Sound & Light show at Jaisalmer War Museum. Overnight at desert camp.

Extra Topping : Soft Drink at Desert Camp, Jaisalmer. Tea/Coffee at Jaisalmer Fort.

Breakfast
Lunch
Dinner
5Desert camp Jaisalmer â€“ Jodhpur
Morning visit Jaisalmer War museum. Proceed to Jodhpur â€“ Positioned in the Thar Desert's stark landscape, Jodhpur is also know as the â€˜Blue cityâ€™ of Rajasthan. On arrival at Jodhpur enjoy free time for shopping.

Extra Topping : Tea/ Coffee en route to Jodhpur

6Jodhpur
City tour includes visit to Ummaid Bhavan Palace Museum - a magnificent piece of Rajasthan's heritage, and a symbol of new Jodhpur, Mehrangarh Fort - one of the largest forts in Rajasthan, Mehrangarh Fort holds the pride of place in Jodhpur because of its splendid architecture and the diverse history associated with it. The fort covers an area of 1200 acres and is built on 125 m high hill. Here we visit various mahals of Mehrangarh fort like Moti Mahal, Phool Mahal, Sheesh Mahal, Silah Khana, Daulat Khana and Rang Mahal. Later visit Jaswant Thada â€“ a cenotaph built in the memory of Maharaja Jaswant Singh.. Enjoy get together with your travel companions in the evening.

Extra Topping : Kachori at Jodhpur.
